[LLM ANSWER]
Here's an initial draft for you:

**End-of-Working Relationship Questionnaire**

As we continue striving towards excellence, it is essential that our employees have positive and productive experiences. To better understand your journey with us as well-rounded individuals leave their roles at [Company Name], this questionnaire aims to gain valuable insights into the end of working relationship.

Please take a few minutes (about 10-15) from now on!

**Section A: Reflections**

1a.) What was most memorable about my time spent in our organization?

(Remember, there's no right or wrong answer! We want your honest reflections.)

2. How would you describe the overall experience of working with [Company Name]?
(Choose one that best represents):
   Very Positive
    Somewhat Neutral 
     Not Too Satisfied

3a.) What were some significant accomplishments during my tenure? (Please specify)

**Section B: Reasons for Leaving**

1b.). Why did I decide to leave the organization?

(Please select all applicable reasons from below. If none apply, please describe your reason.)

* Lack of professional growth opportunities
    Burnout or excessive workload 
     New job opportunity with better compensation/scope/flexibility    
      Other (please specify)

2a.) Were there any specific events/ incidents that contributed to my decision?

(Please provide details if yes. If no skip this question!)

**Section C: Feedback & Suggestions**

1c.). What do I think [Company Name] excelled at during our time together? 

(Share your appreciation, and we'll take it as a compliment)

2a.) Are there any areas where you believe the organization could improve?

(Please provide constructive feedback. Your input matters!)

3b). If given an opportunity to suggest changes or improvements for future employees in similar situations:

What would I recommend changing? (Please describe briefly.)

**Section D: Final Thoughts**

1d.). As a departing employee, what advice do you have regarding our organization's culture and work environment?

(Please share your insights. We value this perspective!)

2a.) Any final words of wisdom for the company as we continue to grow/evolve? 

(Your thoughts matter! Take one last chance.)

Thank You!

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Onboarding

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Here is an example questionnnaire for investigating employee experiences during their first few weeks at work, also known as "on-reading":

**Onboarded Employee Questionnaires**

We value your feedback and would like to hear about our new hire's experience. Your responses will help us improve the onboarding process.

Please answer honestly!

1.
How did you find out that [Company Name] was hiring for this role?

a) Job posting online
b ) Referral from a friend or colleague 
c). Company website/job description

2 . What made your want to apply at our company? (Select all the options)

* Mission and values aligned with my own goals/values?
 * Opportunity of growth/development in new skills/knowledge area ?
*. The role itself seemed interesting/challenging ?

3. How would you rate overall satisfaction during onboarding process?

a) Very satisfied
b). Somewhat neutral 
c . Not very much 

4.
What was the most helpful resource or tool provided to aid your understanding of our company policies and procedures? (Select one)

* Orientation sessions/training modules?
*. Company intranet/wiki ?
 *. Supervisor/mentor guidance

5. How would you rate communication from HR/recruitment team during onboarding?

a) Excellent
b). Good 
c . Fair/Poor 

6.
What was the most significant challenge faced while adapting to new work environment? (Select one)

* Technical difficulties with software/hardware?
*. Unclear job expectations/tasks ?
 *. Difficulty connecting/communicating effectively ?

7. How would you rate support from colleagues in your team during onboarding?

a) Very helpful
b). Somewhat neutral 
c . Not very much 

8.
What suggestions do have for improving the overall new hire experience? (Open-ended text field)

**Thank You!**

Your input is invaluable to us!

Please let me know if you want this questionnaire in a different format, such as multiple-choice questions or Likert scales.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Onboarding

[LLM ANSWER]
Here is an initial draft for you:

**Manager Feedback Questionnaire**

As part our ongoing efforts in improving management practices, we would like gather insights from your perspective as managers to better understand what works well and where improvements can be made. Your input will help us tailor training programs & resources that meet the unique needs of each manager.

Please take a few minutes (about 10-15 questions) share with you:

**Section A: Overall Satisfaction**

1a.) On average, how satisfied are your team members when it comes to working under my leadership? 
(Scale - Very Satisfied =5 , Somewhat Unsatisfactory=2)

How do I improve?

[Insert text box for managers' suggestions]

---

Please provide any additional comments about what you like/dislike most as a manager.

**Section B: Communication**

1b.) How often would your team members agree that we have regular and open communication? 
(Scale - Almost Always =5 , Rarely=2)

What are some effective ways I can improve my verbal/non-verbal cues?

[Insert text box for managers' suggestions]

---

Do you find it challenging to effectively communicate goals, expectations & feedback with your team members?
Yes/No

If Yes: Please describe the challenges and suggest how we could better support.

  }
}
```

Note that I've used the `1` type for all questions, assuming that you want to allow the respondent to choose one answer from a list. If you want to allow multiple answers, you would use the `2` type.

**Feedback Mechanics: Enhancing Open Communication**

We want you! Your input is invaluable in helping us refine our internal communication channels. Please take 5 minutes to share your thoughts and opinions.

1\. How often do **you currently receive constructive criticism or positive reinforcement from supervisors, peers**, &/or colleagues? (Scale of Frequency)

b) Weekly/Monthly 
c Rare

2 What are the most effective ways you've received feedback in our organization?

	+ Not at all confident
    + Somewhat unconfident 
     Unlikely, but possible if they improve
    
2-3 times a year (Not often)
 4 or more time per quarter. Regularly.

   Never makes them on their own
    Sometimes follows the advice of others 
     Makes some, but not all
    
1-2 times a year (Not often)
 3 or more time per quarter. Regularly.
    
* How would rate your leader in terms managing and leading change initiatives?

(5-point scale: Strong disagreement to strong agreement)

Section B - Communication Styles

Which of the following statements best describes how [Leader's Name] communicates with their team?
   Clearly, concisely & consistently
    Sometimes clear but not always consistent 
     Not very often or unclear
    
How would you rate your leader in terms listening actively and responding thoughtfully?

(5-point scale: Strong disagreement to strong agreement)

Section C. Leadership Style

   A transformational – inspiring & empowering
    An operational - efficient, effective 
     Transactionally focused on tasks
    
How would you rate your leader in terms building trust with their team?

(5-point scale: Strong disagreement to strong agreement)

Section D. Feedback and Coaching

* How often do receive feedback from [Leader's Name]?
   Rarely – less than 1 time per month
    Occasionally - between once a week & monthly
    
How would you rate your leader in terms of providing constructive coaching?

(5-point scale: Strong disagreement to strong agreement)

Section E. Collaboration and Teamwork

To what extent do believe [Leader's Name] fosters collaboration among team members?
   Rarely – less than 1 time per month
    Occasionally - between once a week & monthly
    
How would you rate your leader in terms of supporting teamwork?

(5-point scale: Strong disagreement to strong agreement)

**Introduction:**
Thank you taking time to participate in this survey. Your feedback will help us understand how we can improve the new hire experience and ensure a smooth transition into your role.

### Section 1 - Pre-Onboarding Experience

* I received all necessary information about my job responsibilities, expectations & goals. [Scale: Not at All Relevant to Extremely Relevant]

	+ Email
    + Phone call with HR/Manager/Director

[Open-ended text box for respondents' feedback]

    + HR/Manager/Director briefings

[Open-ended text box for respondents' feedback]

### Section 3 - Managerial Support & Feedback

	+ Daily
    + Weekly

    + HR/Manager/Director support
